                            KUSALATTIKAṂ 
                           PAṬICCAVĀRO 
                          A  PAṆṆATTIVĀRO   
                    Hetupaccayo   a  Anulomaṃ   
       i  Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo 
 uppajjeyya hetupaccayā   
       ii  Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo 
 uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
       iii  Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo 
 uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
       iv        kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
       v        akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
       vi        kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
       vii        kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ 
 hetupaccayā  
       viii  Siyā akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            a  akusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            b  kusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            c  avyākato dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
      Siyā akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            d  akusalo ca avyākato ca  dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            e  kusalo ca avyākato ca  dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            f  kusalo ca akusalo ca  dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            g  kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
       ix  Siyā avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            a  avyākato dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            b  kusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            c  akusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
      Siya avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            d  kusalo ca avyākato ca  dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            e  akusalo ca avyākato ca  dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            f  kusalo ca akusalo ca  dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            g  kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
                                                                            Udāhu pañhavāro  udāhu pucchāvāro  Comy  
   Such of these possible relations as actually occur are answered 
 affirmatively in the Niddesavāro  p      
  
  
  page      
                        Kusalattikaṃ 
       x  Siyā kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            a  kusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            b  akusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            c  avyākato dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            d  kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            e  akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            f  kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            g  kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākatā ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
       xi  Siyā akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            a  kusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            b  akusalo dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            c  avyākato dhammo  uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
            d  kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            e  akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            f  kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
            g  kusalo ca akusalo ca  avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā  
      Siyā kusalañ ca akusalañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            a   g  as above  
      Siyā kusalañ ca akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca 
            a   g  as above  
                                   
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 ārammaṇapaccayā        
      Yathā hetupaccayo vitthārito  Evaṃ ārammaṇapaccayo 
 pi vitthāretabbo vācanā maggena       evaṃ adhipatipaccayo 
       avigatapaccayo pi vitthāretabbo vācanā maggena  
                           Ekamūlakaṃ  
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā       pe       hetupaccayā 
 avigatapaccayā   
                           Dumūlakaṃ  
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā       pe       
 hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā avigatapaccayā  
                           Timūlakaṃ  
  
  page      
                           Paṭiccavāro                             
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetu   ārammaṇa   adhipati   anantarapaccayā       
 pe       hetu   ārammaṇa   adhipati   avigatapaccayā  
                           Catumūlakaṃ  
      Pañcamūlamūkādikā saṅkhittā  Ekamūlakaṃ  dumūlakaṃ  
 ti   catu   pañca   sabbamūlakaṃ asaṃmuyhantena vitthāretabbaṃ  
                           Hetumūlakaṃ  
                                      
      So for the other paccayas         
      Ekekassa padassa ekamūlakaṃ  dumūlakaṃ  timūlakaṃ  
 catumūlakaṃ  pañcamūlakaṃ  sabbamūlakaṃ asaṃmuyhantena 
 vitthāretabbaṃ  
           Tikañ ca paṭṭhānavaraṃ dukuttamaṃ 
           Dukaṃ tikañ ceva tikaṃ dukañ ca 
           Tikaṃ tikañ ceva dukaṃ dukañ ca 
           Cha anulomamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti  
                           b  Paccanīyaṃ   
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 na hetupaccayā         Yathā anulome hetupaccayo vitthāretabbo  evaṃ paccanīye pi na hetupaccayo vitthāretabbo   
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ       na ārammaṇapaccayā       
 na adhipatipaccayā       pe       no atthipaccayā       nonatthipaccayā       no vigatapaccayā       no avigatapaccayā        
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 na hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā         Yathā anulome ekekassa padassa ekamūlakaṃ  dumūlakaṃ  timūlakaṃ  
 catumūlakaṃ  yāva tevīsatimūlaṃ  evaṃ paccanīye pi vitthāretabbaṃ   
      Tikañ ca        here follows the quatrain as above  substituting cha paccanīyamhi for cha anulomamhi   
  
  page      
                        Kusalattikaṃ 
                       c  Anulomapaccanīyaṃ   
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā       akusalo 
 dhammo uppajjeyya        
       Yathā anulome hetupaccayo vitthārito  evaṃ anulomapaccanīye pi padaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ   
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 hetupaccayā na adhipatipaccayā        hetupaccayā naanantarapaccayā        pe       hetupaccayā no avigatapaccayā        
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya  a  hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā na adhipatipaccayā        na anantarapaccayā         pe       no avigatapaccayā         b  hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā na anantarapaccayā         hetu   ārammaṇaadhipati paccayā no avigatapaccayā        pe       
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya ārammaṇapaccayā       avigatapaccayā         na hetupaccayā       avigatapaccayā         na ārammaṇapaccayā 
       avigatapaccayā no vigatapaccayā       avigatapaccayā 
 hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā       avigatapaccayā  
       hetupaccayā no vigatapaccayā       avigatapaccayā   
       hetu  ārammaṇa paccayā nādhipati paccayā       avigatapaccayā        hetu  ārammaṇa no vigata paccayā       
 avigatapaccayā         hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā       
 pe       no vigatapaccayā        
      Tikañ ca paṭṭhānaṃ       pe          
      Cha anuloma paccanīyamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti  
                       Paccanīyānulomaṃ   
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 na hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā         na hetupaccayā 
 adhipatipaccayā        pe       na hetupaccayā avigatapaccayā        
                                                                            The quatrain as above save in last line  
  
  
  page      
                           Paticcavāro                            
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya na hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā 
       pe       avigatapaccayā        na hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā na adhipatipaccayā       pe       avigatapaccayā        pe       no atthi        no natthi        novigatapaccayā avigatapaccayā         
      Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya 
 nārammaṇapaccayā  hetupaccayā         na ārammaṇapaccayā  adhipatipaccayā        pe       na ārammaṇapaccayā avigatapaccayā        pe       no atthipaccayā 
 hetupaccayā        no avigatapaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā  
       pe       no avigatapaccayā vigatapaccayā        noavigatapaccayā na hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā        
 no avigatapaccayā na hetupaccayā vigatapaccayā        
 no avigatapaccayā na hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā naadhipatipaccayā       pe       no atthipaccayā no natthipaccayā vigatapaccayā  
      Tikañ ca paṭṭhānaṃ        the quatrain as above but  
      Cha paccanīyānulomamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti 
                      Paṇṇattivāro niṭṭhito  
                           B  NIDDESAVĀRO   
                              hetu   
       i   Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā  
           tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho  
           dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā       
       iii  Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato khandho uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ       
                                                                            B  sic 
   Cf  corresponding questions in Paṇṇattivāro  p     f  
  
  
  page      
                             Kusalattikaṃ 
       iv  Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo ca avyākato ca 
 dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
           tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho citta   etc  
           dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā citta   etc  
       viii  a  Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayo  
      Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ        as above   
       viii  c  Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Akusale khandhe paṭicca        as above   
       viii  d  Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo ca avyākato 
 ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Akusalaṃ ekaṃ       tayo       dve        as above   
       ix  a  Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo 
 uppajjeyya hetupaccayā  
      Vipākavyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ tayo 
 khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ       dve khandhe 
 paṭicca dve khandhā citta       pe       
      Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ       tayo khandhe paṭicca 
 eko khandho kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ       dve khandhe paṭicca 
 dve khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ       khandhe paṭicca vatthuṃ 
       vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā       ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo mahabhūtā       tayo mahābhūte paṭicca ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ       dve mahābhūte paṭicca dve mahābhūtā       
 mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ       kaṭattārūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ       
       x  c  Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato 
 dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ 
 rūpaṃ       
       xi  c  Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato 
 dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ

       i  Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati 
 ārammaṇapaccayā        continue as in     
       viii  a  Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati 
 ārammaṇapaccayā  continue as under    viii  a   
       ix  a  Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo 
 uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā  
      Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo khandhā       tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho       
 dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā       
      Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo khandhā       tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho       
 dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā       vatthuṃ paṭicca 
 khandhā       
                                   
       i  Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati 
 adhipatipaccayā        continue as before   
       iii  Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati 
 adhipatipaccayā  
      Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ       
       iv  Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo ca avyākato ca 
 dhammā uppajjanti adhipatipaccayā  
      Kusalaṃ ekaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ       
      Kusalaṃ tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ       
      Kusalaṃ dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ       
       viii  a  Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo 
 uppajjati adhipatipaccayā  
            ekaṃ       tayo       tayo       ekaṃ       dve       
 dve        
       viii  c  Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo 
 uppajjati adhipatipaccayā  
      Akusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  
       viii  d  Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo ca avyākato 
 ca dhammā uppajjanti adhipatipaccayā

                        Kusalattikaṃ 
      Akusalaṃ ekaṃ        as above    c        cittasamuṭṭhānañ 
 ca rūpaṃ  
       ix  a  Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo 
 uppajjati adhipaṭipaccayā  
      Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo khandhā  
           tayo khandhe       eko       samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
           dve khandhe       dve       samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
      Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā       
           tayo mahābhūte paṭicca ekaṃ mahabhūtaṃ       
           dve mahābhūte paṭicca dve mahābhūtā       
 mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ  
       x  c  Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato 
 dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā  
      Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamutthānaṃ 
 rūpaṃ  
       xi  c  Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato 
 dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā  
      Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ       
                                      
       i  Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati 
 anantara paccayā       samanantarapaccayā  
      Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā       
      Anantaraṃ pi samanantaraṃ pi ārammaṇapaccaya sadisaṃ  
                                   
       i  Kusalaṃ       kusalo       uppajjati sahajātapaccayā  
      Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo       
           tayo khandhe paṭicca eko       
           dve khandhe paṭicca dve       
       iii  Kusalaṃ       avyākato       uppajjati sahajātapaccayā  
      Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  
       iv  Kusalaṃ       kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti 
 sahajātapaccayā  
      Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ       tayo cittasamuṭṭhanañ ca rūpaṃ  
           tayo               eko cittasamuṭṭhanañ ca rūpaṃ  
           dve               dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhanañ ca rūpaṃ

                           Paṭiccavāro                            
       viii  a  Akusalaṃ       akusalo       uppajjati sahajātapaccayā  
       viii  b  Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ       tayo       
                          tayo                 eko       
                          dve                 dve khandhā       
       viii  c  Akusalaṃ       avyākato       uppajjati sahajātapaccayā  
      Akusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  
       viii  d  Akusalaṃ       akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā 
 uppajjanti sahajātapaccayā  
      Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ       tayo       cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
           tayo               eko cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
           dve               dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
       ix  a  Avyākataṃ       avyākato       uppajjati sahajātapaccayā  
      Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
           tayo khandhe       eko       cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
           dve khandhe       dve       cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
      Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ       
                 tayo khandhā eko       kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ  
                 dve khandhā dve       kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ  
                 khandhe paṭicca vatthuṃ       
                 vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā  
      Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo       
           tayo           ekaṃ

                            Gaṇanamūlakā  
                         Hetu ekamūlakaṃ   
 Na hetuyā dve       Na H      na kamme tīṇi       Na K    
 na ārammaṇe pañca  Na Ā      na vipāke nava       Na V    
 na adhipatiyā nava  Na A      na indriye ekaṃ      Na I    
 na anantare pañca  Na An      na jhāne ekaṃ       Na Jh    
 na samanantare pañca  Na S      na magge ekaṃ       Na M    
 na aññamaññe pañca  Na Añ      na sampayutte pañca  Na Sp    
 na upanissaye pañca  Na U      na vippayutte tīṇi  Na Vpp    
 na purejāte satta  Na Pu      no natthiyā pañca  No Nat    
 na pacchājāte nava  Na Pa      no vigate pañca      No Vg    
 na āsevane nava       Na Ās      
 Na hetupaccayā 
      Na Ā        Na U            Na V        Na Sp   
      Na A        Na Pu        Na Āh        Na Vpp   
      Na An        Na Pa        Na I        No Nat   
      Na S        Na Ās        Na Jh        No Vg   
      Na Añ        Na K        Na M   
                            Dumūlakaṃ   
 Na hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā 
      Na A    Na An    Na S         pe        as above  but all with only 
 ekaṃ   
                            Ti mūlakādi   
      Na hetupaccayā na ārammaṇapaccayā na adhipaṭipaccayā       and 
 so on to      no vigatapaccayā  omitting                       
                           Na hetumūlakaṃ  
                                                                            From this point the paccayas  when they occur in lists  will be 
      printed in abbreviated form  and the number of cittas  in which 
      they are experienced  in numerals  In this first list they are 
      printed both in full and in abbreviated form  as a guide  The 
      following is a full list of the paccayas and their abbreviations  
    Hutu      H      Upanissaya U       Jhāna      Jh 
    Ārammaṇa Ā       Purejāta Pu       Magga      M 
    Adhipati A       Pacchājāta Pā       Sampayutta Sp 
    Anantara An       Āsevana     Ās       Vippayutta Vpp 
    Samanantara S       Kamma      K       Atthi      At 
    Shajāta Sj       Vipāka      V       Natthi      Nat 
    Aññamañña Añ       Āhāra      Āh       Vigata      Vg 
    Nissaya     N       Indriya      I       Avigata     Avg

 taṃ paccavekkhati  pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati  jhānā

 uppajjati  vicikicchā uppajjati  uddhaccaṃ uppajjati  domanassaṃ uppajjati  pubbe suciṇṇāni assādeti abhinandati

      Kusalo       avyākatassa      ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo

 suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati  kusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati  cetopariyañāṇena kusalacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ 
 jhānāti  sekhā vā puthujjanā vā kusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato 
 anattato vipassanti  kusale niruddhe vipāko tad ārammaṇatā 
 uppajjati  kusalaṃ assādeti abhinandati  taṃ ārabbha rāgo 
 uppajjati  diṭṭhi uppajjati  vicikicchā uppajjati  uddhaccaṃ 
 uppajjati  domanassaṃ uppajjati  akusale niruddhe vipāko 
 tad ārammaṇatā uppajjati

      Kusalo dhammo kusalassa       vigatap  paccayo  
      Purimā purimā kusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ 
 kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ vipākapaccayena paccayo         Sankhittaṃ  Yathā anantarapaccayaṃ evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ  
                                    
      Kusalo dhammo kusalassa       avigatap  paccayo  
      Kusalo eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ       dvinnaṃ 
 khandhānaṃ avigatapaccayena paccayo        Sankhittaṃ

            Pañhāvārassa paccanīya uddhāraṃ    
 Kusalo dhammo  a  kusalassa dhammassa 
           ārammaṇa paccayena paccayo  
           sahajāta paccayena paccayo  
           upanissaya paccayena paccayo  
 Kusalo dhammo  b  akusalassa dhammassa 
           ārammaṇa paccayena paccayo  
           upanissaya paccayena paccayo  
 Kusalo dhammo  c  avyākatassa dhammassa 
           ārammaṇa paccayena paccayo  
            sahajāta   paccayena paccayo  
           upanissaya paccayena paccayo  
           pacchājāta paccayena paccayo  
           kamma paccayena paccayo  
 Kusalo dhammo  d  kusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa sahajata paccayena paccayo  
 Akusalo dhammo  a  akulassa dhammassa        d         these correspond to  a   d  above  substituting kusalo for akusalo and v v    
                                                                            See below p       Cf  Comy  hereon  
   K  omits  
  
  
  page      
                           Pañhavāro                         
 Avyākato dhammo  a  avyākatassa dhammassa 
           ārammaṇa paccayena paccayo  
           sahajāta paccayena paccayo  
           upanissaya paccayena paccayo  
           purejāta paccayena paccayo  
           pacchājāta paccayena paccayo  
           āhāra paccayena paccayo  
           kamma paccayena paccayo  
 Avyākato dhammo  b  kusalassa dhammassa 
           ārammaṇa paccayena paccayo  
           upanissaya paccayena paccayo  
           purejāta paccayena paccayo  
 Avyākato dhammo  c  akusalassa dhammassa 
                           as for  b

           sahajātaṃ  purejātaṃ  
           sahajātaṃ  pacchājātaṃ  āhāraṃ  indriyaṃ  c      
 Akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā  a        
                           as for  c  above

                           as for  c  above
